                </script></div></div><div class="media__copyright " data-nosnippet=""><div class="media__copyright-item m-copyright">© Photo : Senior Airman Erin Piazza</div></div></div></div><div class="article__news-services-subscribe" data-modal-open="subscribe"><span class="article__news-services-subscribe-label">Subscribe</span><ul class="article__news-services-subscribe-list"><li class="article__news-services-subscribe-item social-service" title="Telegram" data-name="telegram"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#telegram"></use></svg></li><li class="article__news-services-subscribe-item social-service" title="X" data-name="twitter"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#twitter"></use></svg></li></ul></div><div class="article__author the-in-carousel__ready"><div class="the-in-carousel the-in-carousel__1744370915089 the-in-carousel__ready"><iframe title="frame" name="the-in-carousel__1744370915089" class="the-in-carousel__size-frame"></iframe><div class="the-in-carousel__stage"><div class="the-in-carousel__frame"><div class="the-in-carousel__pack" style="padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; width: 300px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; left: 0px;"><div class="the-in-carousel__item m-active" data-item="1" style="margin-right: -1px; width: 300px;"><div class="article__author-item"><div class="article__author-wrapper"><div class="article__author-info"><div class="article__author-name">Gaby Arancibia </div><div class="article__author-links"><a class="m-color-main" href="/author_gaby_arancibia/" title="All materials">All materials</a><a data-modal-open="feedback_author" href="mailto:g.arancibia@sputniknews.com" title="Write to the author">Write to the author</a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article__announce-text">Since the onset of the COVID-19 pandemic, the US has reported upwards of 32 million COVID-19 cases and nearly 576,000 deaths, according to figures released by Johns Hopkins University. To date, an estimated 240 million vaccines have been administered, as roughly 102 million Americans have been fully vaccinated.</div></div><div class="article__body"><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text"><p>US President Joe Biden recently commented that the decision to mandate all US troops to vaccinate against SARS-CoV-2, the deadly virus that causes COVID-19, will be left up to military leadership.</p>
<p>Biden declared during a <a href="https://twitter.com/TODAYshow/status/1388089489826975754?s=20" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="link_tw">Friday interview</a> with NBC News’ Craig Melvin that while he has not ruled out the possibility of requiring all US soldiers to subject themselves to one of the approved COVID-19 vaccines, it would be a “tough call” to make.</p>
<blockquote class="marker-quote1">“I don’t know. I’m going to leave that to the military,” Biden told Melvin after being asked whether a vaccine mandate would be issued for American forces. “I’m not saying I won’t. I think you’re going to see more and more of them getting it.”</blockquote>
<p>“I think it’s going to be a tough call as to whether or not they should be required to have to get it in the military, because you’re in such close proximity with other military personnel - whether you’re in a quarters, where you’re all sleeping, or whether you’re out in maneuvers,” he added.</p>
<blockquote class="marker-quote1">At present, the vaccine is being administered to troops on a voluntary basis since the vaccines are only being dispersed on an emergency use authorization from the US Food and Drug Administration, as opposed to having been granted full approval from the agency.</blockquote>
<p>John Kirby, press secretary for the Pentagon, <a href="https://www.military.com/daily-news/2021/03/01/military-may-revisit-making-covid-19-vaccines-mandatory-after-fda-grants-approval.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">confirmed</a> in March that the military brass was weighing whether to make the vaccinations mandatory.</p></div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">
<p>The commander-in-chief’s comments came as the US Department of Defense sounded off about troops not wanting to vaccinate themselves against the novel coronavirus. Maj. Gen. Jeff Taliaferro, who serves as the vice director of operations for the Joint Staff, <a href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/02/17/troops-covid-vaccine-pentagon-469518" target="_blank" rel="noopener">told lawmakers</a> during a mid-February hearing with the House Armed Services Committee that one-third of soldiers were not interested in the vaccine.</p>
<blockquote class="marker-quote1">More recently, figures released by the US Marine Corps revealed that nearly 40% of Marines who were offered a COVID-19 vaccine by the Pentagon turned the opportunity down. The Marine Corp Times <a href="https://www.marinecorpstimes.com/news/your-marine-corps/2021/04/14/nearly-40-percent-of-marines-have-turned-down-covid-19-vaccine-from-the-corps/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">reported</a> in mid-April that about 48,000 Marines declined, whereas at least 75,000 service members have had at least a partial dose.</blockquote>
<p>While the Pentagon does not have a system in place to offer exact figures on service members who have opted out of being vaccinated, US Army Lt. Gen. Ronald J. Place, who serves as the director of the Defense Health Agency,<a href="https://www.defense.gov/Explore/News/Article/Article/2552011/entire-force-may-be-vaccinated-for-covid-19-by-early-summer/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> remarked</a> to the press in March that every person within the Defense Department could be vaccinated by early summer, should supply rates stand.</p></div></div></div><div class="article__footer"><div class="article__share"><div class="article__sharebar" data-nosnippet=""><span class="share m-article m-active" data-id="1082775132" Defense Ministry"></a><div itemprop="headline">Russian Forces Carry Out 8 Mass Strikes on Ukraine Military Facilities - Defense Ministry</div><div itemprop="name">Russian Forces Carry Out 8 Mass Strikes on Ukraine Military Facilities - Defense Ministry</div><div itemprop="alternateName">Sputnik International</div><div itemprop="description">The Russian military carried out eight group strikes in the past week on the infrastructure of the armed forces of Ukraine, the Russian Defense Ministry said on Friday. </div><div itemprop="datePublished">2025-04-11T11:17+0000</div><div itemprop="dateCreated">2025-04-11T11:17+0000</div><div itemprop="dateModified">2025-04-11T11:17+0000</div><div itemprop="articleSection">russia's special operation in ukraine</div><div itemprop="articleSection">ukrainian crisis</div><div itemprop="articleSection">russian defense ministry</div><div itemprop="articleSection">ukraine</div><div itemprop="associatedMedia">https://cdn1.img.sputnikglobe.com/img/07e8/07/03/1119232130_0:41:3567:2047_1920x0_80_0_0_da0362961e44ddbb4e5439624082c9ab.jpg</div><div itemprop="articleBody">"On April 5-11 this year, the armed forces of Russia carried out eight group strikes with high-precision long-range air and sea-based weapons, unmanned aerial vehicles, as a result of which the infrastructure of military airfields, enterprises of the military-industrial complex of Ukraine, assembly workshops, storage sites for unmanned aerial vehicles, ammunition depots, as well as points of temporary deployment of Ukrainian armed formations and foreign mercenaries were destroyed," the statement said. Russia's Tsentr group of forces has eliminated more than 3,005 Ukrainian soldiers over the past week, the ministry said, adding that the Yug group has eliminated up to 2,085 Ukrainian soldiers. The Zapad group of the Russian forces has eliminated more than 1,585 Ukrainian military personnel, while the Sever group of forces eliminated over 2,345 Ukrainian soldiers in the past week, the ministry said. Russia's Vostok group has eliminated over 1,060 soldiers in battles in the past week, the statement read.</div><div The Russian military carried out eight group strikes in the past week on the infrastructure of the armed forces of Ukraine, the Russian Defense Ministry said on Friday. </div></div><div class="article__body"><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">"On April 5-11 this year, the armed forces of Russia carried out eight group strikes with high-precision long-range air and sea-based weapons, unmanned aerial vehicles, as a result of which the infrastructure of military airfields, enterprises of the military-industrial complex of Ukraine, assembly workshops, storage sites for unmanned aerial vehicles, ammunition depots, as well as points of temporary deployment of Ukrainian armed formations and foreign mercenaries were destroyed," the statement said. </div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="article" data-article="main-photo"><div class="article__article m-image"><a href="/20250410/russian-strikes-obliterate-ukraines-top-artillery-munitions-plants-the-details-1121852491.html" class="article__article-image" inject-number="1" inject-position="" title="Russian Strikes Obliterate Ukraine’s Top Artillery Munitions Plants: The Details"><img media-type="ar10x4" data-source-sid="ap_photo" alt=" - forces has eliminated</a> more than 1,585 Ukrainian military personnel, while the Sever group of forces eliminated over 2,345 Ukrainian soldiers in the past week, the ministry said. </div></div><div He has spoken about this more than once even before the start of the special military operation ... Well, can such a person [Zelensky] even hypothetically think about giving up these people? No way and never. And this understanding is also shared by the Trump administration, which has publicly said more than once that Zelensky will have to come to terms with the territorial issue as well," Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting.On Recent Prisoner Swap The idea of ​​a prisoner exchange between Russia and the United States, which took place on the day of negotiations between the two countries in Istanbul on April 10, was initiated simultaneously on both sides, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday.The prisoner exchange between Moscow and Washington is helping to build trust, but it will take a long time to finally restore it, the minister said.Russia's contacts with US President Donald Trump's team showed that there is a fundamental understanding of the need for dialogue, Lavrov said, adding that such an approach is possible.Sanctions Relief Possibility Russia has proposed to the US to remove Aeroflot from sanctions list, but there has been no response yet, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday, adding that the resumption of direct flights should be a consequence of lifting sanctions on Aeroflot.During the second round of consultations between Russia and the United States in Istanbul, experts from the Russian side recalled this proposal, the minister said.On Victory Day Parade Russia expects that all heads of the CIS member states will attend the victory day parade in Moscow on May 9, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday.CIS Counterparts Aware of the Course of Russia-US Talks Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday that he had informed the CIS member states' foreign minister about contacts between Russia and the United States, including on Ukraine.Russia sees that the US, unlike Europe, wants to understand the root causes of the Ukraine crisis, the minister added.</div><div itemprop="copyrightHolder" itemscope=""                 </script></div></div></div></div><div class="article__news-services-subscribe" data-modal-open="subscribe"><span class="article__news-services-subscribe-label">Subscribe</span><ul class="article__news-services-subscribe-list"><li class="article__news-services-subscribe-item social-service" title="Telegram" data-name="telegram"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#telegram"></use></svg></li><li class="article__news-services-subscribe-item social-service" title="X" data-name="twitter"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#twitter"></use></svg></li></ul></div><div class="article__announce-text">US President Donald Trump administration understands that Volodymyr Zelensky will have to accept territorial losses, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday. </div></div><div class="article__body"><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">"Returning to the 1991 borders, as Zelensky still demands, is impossible ... He has spoken about this more than once even before the start of the special military operation ... Well, can such a person [Zelensky] even hypothetically think about giving up these people? No way and never. And this understanding is also shared by the Trump administration, which has publicly said more than once that Zelensky will have to come to terms with the territorial issue as well," Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="h3"><div class="article__block-anchor" id="1121856466-1121856637"></div><h3 class="article__h2" id="1121856466-1">On Recent Prisoner Swap </h3></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">The idea of ​​a prisoner exchange between Russia and the United States, which took place on the day of negotiations between the two countries in Istanbul on April 10, was initiated simultaneously on both sides, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="quote"><div class="article__quote"><div class="article__quote-bg"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#quotes"></use></svg><div class="article__quote-bg-line"></div></div><div class="article__quote-text">"The idea was born simultaneously on both sides, I am sure that any humanitarian gesture, even when it comes to two people being reunited with their families, is always positive," Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting.</div><div class="article__quote-info"><div class="elem-info"><div class="elem-info__share"><div class="share" data-id="1121856466" data-url="https://sputnikglobe.com/20250411/team-trump-aware-ukraine-will-have-to-accept-territorial-losses---russias-top-diplomat-1121856466.html?share-block=1121856639" data-title="&quot;The idea was born simultaneously on both sides, I am sure that any humanitarian gesture, even when it comes to two people being reunited with their families, is always positive,&quot; Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting."></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">The prisoner exchange between Moscow and Washington is helping to build trust, but it will take a long time to finally restore it, the minister said.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">Russia's contacts with US President Donald Trump's team showed that there is a fundamental understanding of the need for dialogue, Lavrov said, adding that such an approach is possible.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="quote"><div class="article__quote"><div class="article__quote-bg"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#quotes"></use></svg><div class="article__quote-bg-line"></div></div><div class="article__quote-text">"I think we should not delude ourselves. But aiming for normalization based on mutual recognition and respect for the national interests of each country is entirely realistic and necessary," Lavrov said.</div><div class="article__quote-info"><div class="elem-info"><div class="elem-info__share"><div class="share" data-id="1121856466" data-url="https://sputnikglobe.com/20250411/team-trump-aware-ukraine-will-have-to-accept-territorial-losses---russias-top-diplomat-1121856466.html?share-block=1121856642" data-title="&quot;I think we should not delude ourselves. But aiming for normalization based on mutual recognition and respect for the national interests of each country is entirely realistic and necessary,&quot; Lavrov said."></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="h3"><div class="article__block-anchor" id="1121856466-1121856643"></div><h3 class="article__h2" id="1121856466-2">Sanctions Relief Possibility </h3></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">Russia has proposed to the US to remove Aeroflot from sanctions list, but there has been no response yet, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday, adding that the resumption of direct flights should be a consequence of lifting sanctions on Aeroflot.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="quote"><div class="article__quote"><div class="article__quote-bg"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#quotes"></use></svg><div class="article__quote-bg-line"></div></div><div class="article__quote-text">"It [the resumption of direct flights] will not entail, it should be a consequence of Aeroflot being removed from sanctions list. We made such a proposal before the aforementioned meeting in Riyadh more than a month ago. The Americans accepted it. So far, we have not seen any reciprocal steps," Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting, commenting on whether the resumption of air traffic would entail the lifting of sanctions against Aeroflot.</div><div class="article__quote-info"><div class="elem-info"><div class="elem-info__share"><div class="share" data-id="1121856466" data-url="https://sputnikglobe.com/20250411/team-trump-aware-ukraine-will-have-to-accept-territorial-losses---russias-top-diplomat-1121856466.html?share-block=1121856518" data-title="&quot;It [the resumption of direct flights] will not entail, it should be a consequence of Aeroflot being removed from sanctions list. We made such a proposal before the aforementioned meeting in Riyadh more than a month ago. The Americans accepted it. So far, we have not seen any reciprocal steps,&quot; Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting, commenting on whether the resumption of air traffic would entail the lifting of sanctions against Aeroflot."></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">During the second round of consultations between Russia and the United States in Istanbul, experts from the Russian side recalled this proposal, the minister said.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="quote"><div class="article__quote"><div class="article__quote-bg"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#quotes"></use></svg><div class="article__quote-bg-line"></div></div><div class="article__quote-text">"I have not had a chance to contact them yet. Maybe there have been some developments, but we do not know about them yet. But we will work on this, because this is a return to normality," Lavrov said.</div><div class="article__quote-info"><div class="elem-info"><div class="elem-info__share"><div class="share" data-id="1121856466" data-url="https://sputnikglobe.com/20250411/team-trump-aware-ukraine-will-have-to-accept-territorial-losses---russias-top-diplomat-1121856466.html?share-block=1121856520" data-title="&quot;I have not had a chance to contact them yet. Maybe there have been some developments, but we do not know about them yet. But we will work on this, because this is a return to normality,&quot; Lavrov said."></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="h3"><div class="article__block-anchor" id="1121856466-1121856618"></div><h3 class="article__h2" id="1121856466-3">On Victory Day Parade </h3></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">Russia expects that all heads of the CIS member states will attend the victory day parade in Moscow on May 9, Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="quote"><div class="article__quote"><div class="article__quote-bg"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#quotes"></use></svg><div class="article__quote-bg-line"></div></div><div class="article__quote-text">"All leaders of CIS countries have been invited by President [of Russia Vladimir] Putin to participate in the parade and other events in Moscow, and we expect all of them to be with us on Red Square," Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting.</div><div class="article__quote-info"><div class="elem-info"><div class="elem-info__share"><div class="share" data-id="1121856466" data-url="https://sputnikglobe.com/20250411/team-trump-aware-ukraine-will-have-to-accept-territorial-losses---russias-top-diplomat-1121856466.html?share-block=1121856619" data-title="&quot;All leaders of CIS countries have been invited by President [of Russia Vladimir] Putin to participate in the parade and other events in Moscow, and we expect all of them to be with us on Red Square,&quot; Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting."></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="h3"><div class="article__block-anchor" id="1121856466-1121856723"></div><h3 class="article__h2" id="1121856466-4">CIS Counterparts Aware of the Course of Russia-US Talks </h3></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">Russian Foreign Minister Sergey Lavrov said on Friday that he had informed the CIS member states' foreign minister about contacts between Russia and the United States, including on Ukraine.</div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="quote"><div class="article__quote"><div class="article__quote-bg"><svg class="svg-icon"><use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="/i/sprites/package/inline.svg?63#quotes"></use></svg><div class="article__quote-bg-line"></div></div><div class="article__quote-text">"I spoke with our colleagues, shared with them some details of our contacts with the Americans, at various levels, including on issues of Washington's assistance in resolving the Ukrainian crisis, [US] President [Donald] Trump emphasizes his interest in this each time," Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting.</div><div class="article__quote-info"><div class="elem-info"><div class="elem-info__share"><div class="share" data-id="1121856466" data-url="https://sputnikglobe.com/20250411/team-trump-aware-ukraine-will-have-to-accept-territorial-losses---russias-top-diplomat-1121856466.html?share-block=1121856725" data-title="&quot;I spoke with our colleagues, shared with them some details of our contacts with the Americans, at various levels, including on issues of Washington's assistance in resolving the Ukrainian crisis, [US] President [Donald] Trump emphasizes his interest in this each time,&quot; Lavrov told reporters following the CIS Foreign Ministers' Council meeting."></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="article__block" data-type="text"><div class="article__text">Russia sees that the US, unlike Europe, wants to understand the root causes of the Ukraine crisis, the minister added.</div></div></div><div class="article__footer"><div class="article__share"><div class="article__sharebar" data-nosnippet=""><span class="share m-article m-active" data-id="1121856466"
